“You couldn’t keep your mouth shut, could you, Hermione?” said Ron angrily as the kitchen door slammed shut behind them. “They won’t want us visiting them now! We could’ve tried to get more stuff out of Winky about Crouch!”

“Oh as if you care about that!” scoffed Hermione. “You only like coming down here for the food!”

It was an irritable sort of day after that. Harry got so tired of Ron and Hermione sniping at each other over their homework in the common room that he took Sirius’s food up to the Owlery that evening on his own.

## Pigwidgeon's Ham Delivery and Evening Observations

**Pigwidgeon** was much too small to carry an entire **ham** up the mountain alone, so **Harry** enlisted the help of two school **screech owls**. They set off into the dusk, looking oddly conspicuous with the large package.

Harry leaned on the windowsill, observing the grounds, the dark, rustling treetops of the **Forbidden Forest**, and the **Durmstrang ship**. An **eagle owl** flew through smoke rising from **Hagrid’s chimney**, soaring toward the castle and disappearing.

Harry noticed **Hagrid** digging energetically in front of his cabin, possibly making a new **vegetable patch**. **Madame Maxime** emerged from the **Beauxbatons carriage** and attempted to engage Hagrid. He seemed reluctant, and she soon returned to the carriage.

Unwilling to endure Ron and Hermione’s quarrels in **Gryffindor Tower**, Harry watched Hagrid until darkness enveloped him and owls around Harry woke and flew into the night.

---

## Breakfast and Incoming Mail Drama

By breakfast, **Ron** and **Hermione’s** bad moods had lifted. Ron’s gloomy prediction that house-elves would send poor quality food, due to Hermione’s insults, proved false; the **bacon, eggs, and kippers** were as good as usual.

When the **post owls** arrived, Hermione eagerly anticipated something.

- Ron explained **Percy** wouldn’t have replied yet since they had only sent **Hedwig** the previous day.
- Hermione revealed she subscribed to the **Daily Prophet**, tired of learning news from the **Slytherins**.
- A gray owl landed with four barn owls, a brown owl, and a tawny, all delivering letters.

Hermione, overwhelmed, opened one letter: it was not handwritten but composed of cut-out letters from the **Daily Prophet** reading:

**"YOU ARE A WICKED GIRL. HARRY POTTER DESERVES BETTER. GO BACK WHERE YOU CAME FROM MUGGLE."**

Hermione opened more letters filled with hateful messages such as:

- **“Harry Potter can do much better than the likes of you…”**
- **“You deserve to be boiled in frog spawn…”**

The last envelope contained **undiluted bubotuber pus**, which spilled on Hermione’s hands, causing large yellow boils.

Ron identified the substance by smell, and Hermione struggled with pain and swelling. Harry advised her to see the **hospital wing** while they told **Professor Sprout**.

Ron blamed **Rita Skeeter**, warning Hermione not to annoy her. He read one letter threatening a curse from Witch Weekly.

---

## School Day Tension and Care of Magical Creatures Class

Hermione missed **Herbology**. As Harry and Ron left the greenhouse, they saw **Malfoy**, **Crabbe**, **Goyle**, and **Pansy Parkinson** gossiping and taunting Hermione’s upset state.

Harry ignored Pansy’s jibes.

**Hagrid** was waiting outside his cabin with open crates, revealing **nifflers**—small, black creatures with long snouts and flat paw-like hands.

Hagrid explained:

- Nifflers are found in mines and attracted to **sparkly objects**.
- He had buried **gold coins** in a patch of fresh earth.
- The class was to choose a niffler and set them loose to dig up the gold.
- The prize would go to the student whose niffler collected the most coins.

Harry removed his non-working watch and picked a cuddly niffler that sniffed his ear. Hagrid noted Hermione’s absence and Ron explained she was at the hospital wing.

The nifflers caused chaos, diving into the earth and spitting gold coins into students’ hands. Ron’s niffler was especially effective.

---

## Nifflers, Gold, and Personal Conflicts

Ron asked if nifflers could be kept as pets. Hagrid warned they wreck houses and said Ron’s niffler was nearly finished collecting the hundred coins he had buried.

Hermione returned with heavily bandaged hands. Hagrid checked on her condition and comforted her about the hate mail, sharing that he had received insulting letters after **Rita Skeeter** wrote about his mother.

Hagrid advised Hermione to burn any more hateful letters rather than open them.

Harry noted it was the most fun they had in **Care of Magical Creatures**.

Goyle, suspected of trying to steal coins, was caught emptying his pockets. Ron won the prize: a large slab of **Honeydukes chocolate**.

---

## Lunch Conversations and Financial Struggles

At lunch, Ron expressed frustration over missing **leprechaun gold** given to Harry at the **Quidditch World Cup**.

- Ron realized the gold had vanished.
- Harry admitted he hadn’t noticed, distracted by other concerns.
- Ron admitted hating being **poor** and envying others' wealth.
- Hermione tried to cheer him up, reminding him that at least his fingers weren't covered in pus.
- She vowed to get revenge on Skeeter.

---

## Ongoing Harassment and Defense Against the Dark Arts

Hate mail continued for Hermione, including **Howlers** that loudly insulted her at the Gryffindor table.

Even students who hadn’t read Witch Weekly knew about the supposed **Harry–Krum–Hermione** love triangle.

Harry reassured Hermione it would die down if ignored and mentioned people had grown bored of past rumors.

Hermione questioned how Rita Skeeter was intercepting private conversations despite a ban from the grounds.

Hermione stayed after **Defense Against the Dark Arts** class to speak with **Professor Moody** about the matter.

The rigorous class had left students injured; Harry suffered **Twitchy Ears**, needing to cover his ears as he walked away.

## Rita Skeeter and Magical Eavesdropping

“Well, **Rita’s definitely not using an Invisibility Cloak!**” Hermione panted five minutes later, catching up with Harry and Ron in the entrance hall. She pulled Harry’s hand away from one of his wiggling ears so he could hear her. "**Moody says he didn’t see her anywhere near the judges’ table at the second task, or near the lake!**"

- Ron asked, "**Hermione, is there any point in telling you to drop this?**"
- Hermione stubbornly replied, "**No!** I want to know how she heard me talking to Viktor! And how she found out about **Hagrid’s mum**!"
- Harry suggested, "**Maybe she had you bugged.**"
- Ron was confused: "**Bugged? What… put fleas on her or something?**"
- Harry explained about hidden microphones and recording equipment.
- Hermione interrupted: "**Aren’t you two ever going to read *Hogwarts, A History*?**"
- Ron said, "**What’s the point? You know it by heart, we can just ask you.**"
- Hermione added: "**All those substitutes for magic Muggles use—electricity, computers, and radar—go haywire around Hogwarts because there’s too much magic in the air. Rita’s using magic to eavesdrop. If I could just find out what it is... if it’s illegal, I’ll have her...**"
- Ron asked, "**Haven’t we got enough to worry about? Do we have to start a vendetta against Rita Skeeter as well?**"
- Hermione snapped, "**I’m not asking you to help! I’ll do it on my own!**"

She marched back up the marble staircase, clearly headed for the **library**.

Ron joked, "**What’s the betting she comes back with a box of Hate Rita Skeeter badges?**"

---

## Harry, Hermione, and Ron’s Workload and Easter Letters

- Hermione pursued her research on magical eavesdropping alone.
- Harry was amazed she could manage this alongside all their other work.
- Harry worked hard to keep up with homework.
- He sent regular food packages and notes to **Sirius** in a cave in the mountain.
- Nothing unusual had happened; they were still waiting for an answer from **Percy**.

During the Easter holidays:

- **Hedwig** returned with Percy’s letter enclosed in huge Easter egg packages from Mrs. Weasley.
- Harry’s and Ron’s eggs were large and full of homemade toffee.
- Hermione’s egg was small, about the size of a chicken egg.
- Hermione sadly noted, "**Your mum doesn’t read *Witch Weekly*, by any chance, Ron?**"
- Ron replied, "**Yeah, gets it for the recipes.**"

Percy's letter was short and irritated:

> "As I am constantly telling the *Daily Prophet*, Mr. Crouch is taking a well deserved break. He is sending

## Encounter with Mr. Crouch

Mr. **Crouch’s eyes** rolled forward onto **Harry**.  
“Who… you?” he whispered.  

Harry explained, **“I’m a student at the school,”** glancing at **Krum** for support, but Krum appeared very nervous.

- Crouch whispered, “You’re not… his?”  
- Harry replied, “No,” unsure what Crouch meant.  
- Crouch asked, “Dumbledore’s?”  
- Harry confirmed, “That’s right.”

Crouch pulled Harry closer with a powerful grip. Harry tried to escape but failed.

- Crouch demanded, “Warn… Dumbledore…”  
- Harry promised, “I’ll get Dumbledore if you let go of me… just let go, Mr. Crouch…”  

Suddenly, Crouch resumed his conversation with a tree, acting unaware of Harry. He asked for a memo and praised his son for gaining **twelve O.W.L.s**.

Harry instructed Krum, “You stay here with him! I’ll get Dumbledore; I know where his office is.”

- Krum agreed cautiously, observing Crouch’s strange behavior.  
- When Harry tried to leave, Crouch grabbed him again, pleading, “Don’t… leave… me!”  
- Crouch muttered about escaping, warning Dumbledore, and mentioned **Bertha**, **his son**, and **the Dark Lord**.

Harry asked for Krum’s help to get free and promised to return with Dumbledore.

## Searching for Dumbledore

Harry rushed toward the stone gargoyle in the corridor.

- He shouted the password, **“Sher—sherbet lemon!”**  
- The gargoyle did not move, indicating the password had changed.

Suddenly, **Snape** appeared from the hidden staircase.

- Snape asked, “What are you doing here, Potter?”  
- Harry explained about Mr. Crouch and needing to see Dumbledore.  
- Snape refused, saying, “The headmaster is busy.”

Harry insisted, but Snape blocked his way. Then, the wall slid open, revealing **Dumbledore** in green robes.

- Dumbledore asked, “Is there a problem?”  
- Harry hurried to tell him about Crouch in the forest wanting to warn him.  
- Dumbledore responded, “Lead the way,” and followed Harry.

## In the Forest

Harry and Dumbledore moved quickly toward the forest.

- Harry described Crouch's erratic behavior and leaving him with Krum.  
- Dumbledore inquired if anyone else had seen Crouch.  
- Harry said no; only he and Krum were watching after the third task.  

They found **Krum** unconscious on the forest floor; no sign of Mr. Crouch. Dumbledore checked Krum and said he was **stunned**.

- Harry asked whether to call for **Madam Pomfrey**.  
- Dumbledore refused and sent a silver bird-like creature to fetch help.

Dumbledore revived Krum with the spell **“Ennervate.”**

- Krum claimed, “The old madman attacked me! He attacked from behind!”

## Arrival of Help

**Hagrid** arrived, carrying a crossbow, followed by **Moody**.

- Dumbledore requested Hagrid fetch **Professor Karkaroff** and alert Moody.  
- Moody was already present, complaining about his injured leg.

Hagrid hurried away to find Karkaroff, who soon arrived looking pale and agitated.

## Karkaroff’s Accusations

Karkaroff confronted Dumbledore fiercely.

- He accused Dumbledore and the Ministry of unfairly influencing the tournament.  
- He called it **treachery** and claimed the competition was corrupted.  

Hagrid reacted violently, lifting Karkaroff and slamming him against a tree.

- Dumbledore stopped Hagrid, who then released Karkaroff.  
- Hagrid was ordered to escort Harry back to the castle and keep him safe in **Gryffindor Tower**.  
- Harry was told not to send any **owls** until morning.

## Returning to the Castle

Hagrid, Harry, and Fang marched quietly back toward the castle.

- Hagrid expressed anger at Karkaroff’s accusations against Dumbledore.  
- He scolded Harry for wandering off alone with Krum from Durmstrang, warning about potential dangers and Moody’s lessons.

## 29. THE DREAM

“Krum’s all right!” said **Harry** as they climbed the steps into the entrance hall. “He wasn’t trying to jinx me, he just wanted to talk about **Hermione**—”

“I’ll be havin’ a few words with her, an’ all,” said **Hagrid** grimly, stomping up the stairs. “The less you lot ’ave ter do with these **foreigners**, the happier yeh’ll be. Yeh can trust any of ’em.”

“You were getting on all right with **Madame Maxime**,” **Harry** said, annoyed.

“Don’ you talk ter me abou’ her!” said **Hagrid**, and he looked quite frightening for a moment. “I’ve got her number now! Tryin’ ter get back in me good books, tryin’ ter get me ter tell her what’s comin in the **third task**. Ha! You can’ trust any of ’em!”

**Hagrid** was in such a bad mood, **Harry** was quite glad to say good-bye to him in front of the Fat Lady. He clambered through the portrait hole into the common room and hurried straight for the corner where **Ron** and **Hermione** were sitting, to tell them what had happened.

---

### Theories About Mr. Crouch’s Attack

“It comes down to this,” said **Hermione**, rubbing her forehead. “Either **Mr. Crouch** attacked **Viktor**, or somebody else attacked both of them when **Viktor** wasn’t looking.”

“It must’ve been **Crouch**,” said **Ron** at once. “That’s why he was gone when **Harry** and **Dumbledore** got there. He’d done a runner.”

“I don’t think so,” said **Harry**, shaking his head. “He seemed really weak—I don’t reckon he was up to **Disapparating** or anything.”

“You can’t **Disapparate** on the **Hogwarts grounds**, haven’t I told you enough times?” said **Hermione**.

“Okay… how’s this for a theory,” said **Ron** excitedly. “**Krum** attacked **Crouch**—no, wait for it—and then **Stunned** himself!”

“And **Mr. Crouch** evaporated, did he?” said **Hermione** coldly.

“Oh yeah…”

---

### Early Morning Discussion at the Owlery

It was daybreak. **Harry**, **Ron**, and **Hermione** had crept out of their dormitories very early and hurried up to the **Owlery** together to send a note to **Sirius**. All three of them were **puffy eyed** and pale because they had been talking late into the night about **Mr. Crouch**.

“Just go through it again, **Harry**,” said **Hermione**. “What did **Mr. Crouch** actually say?”

“I’ve told you, he wasn’t making much sense,” said **Harry**. “He said he wanted to warn **Dumbledore** about something. He definitely mentioned **Bertha Jorkins**, and he seemed to think she was dead. He kept saying stuff was his fault… He mentioned his son.”

“Well, that was his fault,” said **Hermione** testily.

“He was out of his mind,” said **Harry**. “Half the time he seemed to think his wife and son were still alive, and he kept talking to **Percy** about work and giving him instructions.”

“And… remind me what he said about **You-Know-Who**?” said **Ron** tentatively.

“I’ve told you,” **Harry** repeated dully. “He said he’s getting stronger.”

---

### On the Sanity of Mr. Crouch

There was a pause. Then **Ron** said in a falsely confident voice, “But he was out of his mind, like you said, so half of it was probably just raving…”

“He was sanest when he was trying to talk about **Voldemort**,” said **Harry**, and **Ron** winced at the sound of the name. “He was having real trouble stringing two words together, but that was when he seemed to know where he was, and know what he wanted to do. He just kept saying he had to see **Dumbledore**.”

**Harry** turned away from the window and stared up into the rafters. The many perches were half empty; every now and then, another owl would swoop in through one of the windows, returning from its night’s hunting with a mouse in its beak.

---

### Frustrations and Speculations

“If **Snape** hadn’t held me up,” **Harry** said bitterly, “we might’ve got there in time. ‘The headmaster is busy, Potter… what’s this rubbish, Potter?’ Why couldn’t he have just got out of the way?”

“Maybe he didn’t want you to get there!” said **Ron** quickly. “Maybe—hang on—how fast d’you reckon he could’ve gotten down to the forest? D’you reckon he could’ve beaten you and **Dumbledore** there?”

“Not unless he can turn himself into a bat or something,” said **Harry**.

“Wouldn’t put it past him,” **Ron** muttered.

---

### Seeking Professor Moody

“We need to see **Professor Moody**,” said **Hermione**. “We need to find out whether he found **Mr. Crouch**.”

“If he had the **Marauder’s Map** on him, it would’ve been easy,” said **Harry**.

“Unless **Crouch** was already outside the grounds,” said **Ron**, “because it only shows up to the boundaries, doesn’t—”

“Shh!” said **Hermione** suddenly.

Somebody was climbing the steps up to the **Owlery**. **Harry** could hear two voices arguing.

---

### Encounter with Fred and George

Fred and George burst through the **Owlery** door, freezing at the sight of **Harry**, **Ron**, and **Hermione**.

- **Fred**: “What’re you doing here?”
- **Ron**: “Sending a letter,” said **Harry** and **George** in unison.
- **Hermione**: “What, at this time?”
- **Fred** grinned and made a mock bow: “Fine—we won’t ask you what you’re doing, if you don’t ask us.”

Fred was holding a sealed envelope, but he covered the name on it as **Harry** glanced at it.

---

### Blackmail Joke and Consequences

- “Who’re you blackmailing?” said **Ron**.
- **Fred** and **George** said it was a joke.
- **Fred** warned **Ron** to keep his nose out.
- **Ron** expressed concerns about **Fred** and **George**’s obsession with money and their plans for a joke shop.
- **Hermione** was scared about the consequences of blackmail.
- **Ron** refused to tell **Percy**, fearing **Percy** would turn them in.

---

### Waiting for Class and Meeting Moody

**History of Magic** passed slowly. All three were exhausted and out of focus.

When the bell rang, they found **Professor Moody** leaving the **Dark Arts** classroom. He looked tired with his magical eye drooping.

**Harry** asked Moody if he had found **Mr. Crouch**.

- **Moody** said no.
- He used the **Marauder’s Map** summoned to the forest.
- **Crouch** was not on the map.

---

### Discussion of Mr. Crouch’s Disappearance

**Ron** asked if **Crouch** had **Disapparated**.

- **Hermione** reminded him that **Disapparating** on the grounds is impossible.
- **Moody** praised **Hermione**’s logic and hinted she had potential as an **Auror**.
- They considered the possibility **Crouch** was kidnapped.

---

### Possible Locations and Warnings

- **Ron** wondered if **Crouch** was in **Hogsmeade**.
- **Moody** said he could be anywhere, only certain he’s not at **Hogwarts**.

**Moody** warned the students:

- The **Ministry** was notified.
- **Harry** should focus on the **third task**.

---

### Preparing for the Third Task

**Moody** encouraged **Harry**, recalling his past successes with obstacles like those protecting the **Sorcerer’s Stone**.

He urged the students:

- Help **Harry** practice.
- Stay vigilant: "**Constant vigilance, Potter. Constant vigilance.**"

## Magical Eye and Vigilance

He took another long draw from his **hip flask**, and his **magical eye** swiveled onto the window. The topmost sail of the **Durmstrang ship** was visible through it.

“You two,” counseled **Moody**, his normal eye on **Ron** and **Hermione**, “you stick close to **Potter**, all right? I’m keeping an eye on things, but all the same… you can never have too many eyes out.”

## Sirius’s Owl and Warning

Sirius sent their owl back the very next morning. It fluttered down beside **Harry** at the same moment that a tawny owl landed in front of **Hermione**, clutching a copy of the **Daily Prophet** in its beak. She took the newspaper, scanned the first few pages, said, “Ha! She hasn’t got wind of **Crouch**!” then joined Ron and Harry in reading what Sirius had to say on the mysterious events of the night before last.

**Sirius’s letter:**

- Harry, what do you think you are playing at, walking off into the forest with **Viktor Krum**?
- I want you to swear, by return owl, that you are not going to go walking with anyone else at night.
- There is somebody **highly dangerous** at **Hogwarts**.
- They wanted to stop **Crouch** from seeing **Dumbledore** and you were probably feet away from them in the dark.
- You could have been killed.
- Your name didn’t get into the **Goblet of Fire** by accident.
- If someone’s trying to attack you, they’re on their last chance.
- Stay close to Ron and Hermione, do not leave **Gryffindor Tower** after hours.
- Arm yourself for the **third task**.
- Practice **Stunning** and **Disarming** spells. A few **hexes** wouldn’t go amiss either.
- There’s nothing you can do about **Crouch**.
- Keep your head down and look after yourself.
- I’m waiting for your letter giving me your word you won’t stray out of bounds again.

— **Sirius**

## Harry’s Reaction and Discussion

“Who’s he, to lecture me about being out of bounds?” said Harry in mild indignation as he folded up Sirius’s letter and put it inside his robes. “After all the stuff he did at school!”

“He’s worried about you!” said Hermione sharply. “Just like Moody and Hagrid! So listen to them!”

“No one’s tried to attack me all year,” said Harry. “No one’s done anything to me at all—”

“Except put your name in the **Goblet of Fire**,” said Hermione. “And they must’ve done that for a reason, Harry. **Snuffles** is right. Maybe they’ve been biding their time. Maybe this is the task they’re going to get you.”

“Look,” said Harry impatiently, “let’s say Sirius is right, and someone Stunned **Krum** to kidnap **Crouch**. Well, they would’ve been in the trees near us, wouldn’t they? But they waited till I was out of the way until they acted, didn’t they? So it doesn’t look like I’m their target, does it?”

“They couldn’t have made it look like an accident if they’d murdered you in the forest!” said Hermione. “But if you die during a task—”

“They didn’t care about attacking Krum, did they?” said Harry. “Why didn’t they just polish me off at the same time? They could’ve made it look like Krum and I had a duel or something.”

“Harry, I don’t understand it either,” said Hermione desperately. “I just know there are a lot of odd things going on, and I don’t like it… Moody’s right—Sirius is right—you’ve got to get in training for the **third task**, straight away. And you make sure you write back to Sirius and promise him you’re not going to go sneaking off alone again.”

## Training for the Third Task

The **Hogwarts grounds** never looked more inviting than when Harry had to stay indoors. For the next few days he spent all of his free time either in the **library** with Hermione and Ron, looking up **hexes**, or else in empty classrooms, which they sneaked into to practice.

Harry was concentrating on the **Stunning Spell**, which he had never used before. The trouble was that practicing it involved certain sacrifices on Ron’s and Hermione’s part.

“Can’t we kidnap Mrs. Norris?” Ron suggested on Monday lunchtime as he lay flat on his back in the middle of their Charms classroom, having just been **Stunned** and reawoken by Harry for the fifth time in a row. “Let’s Stun her for a bit. Or you could use **Dobby**, Harry, I bet he’d do anything to help you. I’m not complaining or anything”—he got gingerly to his feet, rubbing his backside—“but I’m aching all over…”

“Well, you keep missing the cushions, don’t you!” said Hermione impatiently, rearranging the pile of cushions they had used for the **Banishing Spell**, which **Flitwick** had left in a cabinet. “Just try and fall backward!”

“Once you’re Stunned, you can’t aim too well, Hermione!” said Ron angrily. “Why don’t you take a turn?”

“Well, I think Harry’s got it now, anyway,” said Hermione hastily. “And we don’t have to worry about **Disarming**, because he’s been able to do that for ages… I think we ought to start on some of these hexes this evening.”

She looked down the list they had made in the library.

“I like the look of this one,” she said, “this **Impediment Curse**. Should slow down anything that’s trying to attack you, Harry. We’ll start with that one.”

The bell rang. They hastily shoved the cushions back into Flitwick’s cupboard and slipped out of the classroom.

“See you at dinner!” said Hermione, and she set off for **Arithmancy**, while Harry and Ron headed toward **North Tower**, and **Divination**.

## Divination Class

Broad strips of dazzling gold sunlight fell across the corridor from the high windows. The sky outside was so brightly blue it looked as though

## Passage from Harry Potter: The Pensive Scene

“**Chocolate Frog!**” he yelled angrily, standing on one leg. “**Sugar Quill! Cockroach Cluster!**” The gargoyle sprang to life and jumped aside. Harry blinked.

“**Cockroach Cluster?**” he said, amazed. “I was only joking…”

He hurried through the gap in the walls and stepped onto the foot of a spiral stone staircase, which moved slowly upward as the doors closed behind him, taking him up to a polished oak door with a brass door knocker.

He could hear voices from inside the office. He stepped off the moving staircase and hesitated, listening.

### Conversation inside the Office

“**Dumbledore, I’m afraid I don’t see the connection, don’t see it at all!**” It was the voice of the **Minister of Magic, Cornelius Fudge**. “**Ludo says Bertha’s perfectly capable of getting herself lost. I agree we would have expected to have found her by now, but all the same, we’ve no evidence of foul play, Dumbledore, none at all. As for her disappearance being linked with Barty Crouch’s!**”

“**And what do you think happened to Barty Crouch, Minister?**” said **Moody’s** growling voice.

“**I see two possibilities, Alastor,**” said Fudge. “**Either

## Trial of Igor Karkaroff

Unlike **Dumbledore**, **Karkaroff** looked much younger; his hair and goatee were black. He was not dressed in sleek f

## The Trial Before the Council of Magical Law

The **Dementors** placed each of the four prisoners in chained chairs on the dungeon floor. Among them were:

- A thickset man staring blankly at **Crouch**
- A thinner, nervous man with darting eyes
- A woman with thick, shining dark hair and heavily hooded eyes, sitting as if her chair were a throne
- A terrified boy in his late teens, shivering with straw-colored hair and milk-white freckled skin

The wispy witch beside Crouch rocked back and forth, whimpering into her handkerchief.

Crouch stood up, his face full of pure **hatred**.

“You have been brought here before the **Council of Magical Law**,” he declared, “so that we may pass judgment on you for a crime so heinous—”

The boy pleaded, “Father… please…”

Crouch continued loudly: 

“We have heard the evidence against you. You stand accused of capturing an **Auror**—**Frank Longbottom**—and subjecting him to the **Cruciatus Curse**, believing he held knowledge of the whereabouts of your exiled master, **He-Who-Must-Not-Be-Named**—”

The boy shrieked, “Father, I didn’t! I swear it!”

Crouch bellowed:

“You are further accused of using the **Cruciatus Curse** on Frank Longbottom’s wife when he did not give you information. You planned to restore **He-Who-Must-Not-Be-Named** to power and resume your violent lives during his strength. I now ask the jury—”

The boy screamed, “Mother! Stop him! I didn’t do it!”

Crouch shouted:

“I now ask the jury to raise their hands if they believe these crimes deserve a life sentence in **Azkaban**!”

In unison, the witches and wizards raised their hands. The crowd clapped with savage triumph. The boy began to scream in despair.

The Dementors returned. The prisoners rose quietly. The woman cried out:

“The **Dark Lord** will rise again, Crouch! Throw us into Azkaban; we will wait! He will come for us and reward us beyond all others! We alone were faithful!”

The boy struggled against the Dementors, but their cold power was draining him. The crowd jeered.

“I’m your son!” he screamed at Crouch.

Crouch roared, “You are no son of mine! I have no son!”

The wispy witch beside Crouch gasped and fainted. Crouch was unmoved.

“Take them away!” he ordered. “May they rot there!”

The boy begged, but was dragged away.

## Transition to Dumbledore’s Office

A quiet voice whispered to **Harry** that it was time to return to **Dumbledore’s office**. Harry felt himself rising as the dungeon dissolved around him. Moments later, he landed in **Dumbledore’s sunlit office**, with the shimmering **Pensieve** in a cabinet before him and **Albus Dumbledore** standing nearby.

Harry apologized for looking in the open cabinet door.

Dumbledore replied kindly, “Curiosity is not a sin. But we should exercise caution with our curiosity.”

## The Pensieve Explained

The **Pensieve** is a stone basin used to examine memories and thoughts. **Dumbledore** explained:

- Sometimes he has too many thoughts and memories crammed into his mind.
- He siphons excess thoughts into the basin for easier examination.
- Patterns and links become clearer in this form.

Harry looked at the swirling silvery white substance, surprised that it contained **Dumbledore’s thoughts**.

Dumbledore added a new strand of thought from his silvery hair, producing images and voices from the basin.

He showed Harry a memory of **Severus Snape**, who whispered about **Karkaroff** and a mysterious connection.

## Memory of Bertha Jorkins

A revolving figure emerged from the Pensieve’s depths—a plump, scowling girl named **Bertha Jorkins** remembered from school.

She complained about being hexed and teasing someone about a secret meeting behind the greenhouses.

Dumbledore asked sadly why she had followed that person in the first place.

## Dumbledore’s Age and Reflection

The silvery light of the Pensieve illuminated Dumbledore’s face, revealing how old he was looking, though Harry had never thought of him as old.

Dumbledore then addressed Harry.

## Harry’s Dream and the Scar Pain

Harry explained he had fallen asleep during **Divination** and dreamt about **Lord Voldemort** torturing **Wormtail**.

Details of the dream:

- Voldemort received a letter stating Wormtail's blunder was repaired and someone was dead.
- Voldemort threatened to feed Harry to a snake beside him.
- The **Cruciatus Curse** was used on Wormtail.
- Harry’s scar hurt painfully, waking him up.

Dumbledore listened quietly.

Harry asked if his scar had hurt at other times.

Dumbledore revealed he had been in contact with **Sirius Black** and knew about Harry’s summer scar pain.

## The Scar’s Meaning

Dumbledore theorized that Harry’s scar hurts when:

- **Voldemort** is near Harry
- Voldemort experiences a strong surge of hatred

This was because the scar was connected by the **curse that failed** and was not ordinary.

Harry questioned whether the dream really happened.

Dumbledore said it was possible, even probable.

Harry remarked he had not seen Voldemort’s body but wondered how Voldemort could hold a wand without a body.

Dumbledore mused, “How indeed…”

## Final Thoughts

Silence fell. Dumbledore continued to add more shining thoughts to the Pensieve, their contents swirling rapidly.

Harry asked if Voldemort was getting stronger.

Dumbledore replied with his characteristic piercing look:

“Once again, Harry, I can only give you my suspicions.”

He sighed deeply, looking older and wearier than ever.

## The Years of Voldemort’s Ascent

“The years of **Voldemort’s ascent to power**,” he said, “were marked with **disappearances**. **Bertha Jorkins** has vanished without a trace in the place where Voldemort was certainly known to be last. **Mr. Crouch** too has disappeared… within these very grounds. And there was a third disappearance, one which the Ministry, I regret to say, do not consider of any importance, for it concerns a **Muggle**. His name was **Frank Bryce**, he lived in the village where Voldemort’s father grew up, and he has not been seen since last August. You see, I read the **Muggle newspapers**, unlike most of my Ministry friends.” Dumbledore looked very seriously at Harry.

“These disappearances seem to me to be linked. The Ministry disagrees—as you may have heard, while waiting outside my office.”

Harry nodded. Silence fell between them again, Dumbledore extracting thoughts every now and then. Harry felt as though he ought to go, but his curiosity held him in his chair.

“Professor?” he said again.

“Yes, Harry?” said Dumbledore.

“Er… could I ask you about… that court thing I was in… in the **Pensieve**?”

“You could,” said Dumbledore heavily. “I attended it many times, but some trials come back to me more clearly than others… particularly now…”

“You know—you know the trial you found me in? The one with **Crouch’s son**? Well…were they talking about **Neville’s parents**?”

Dumbledore gave Harry a very sharp look. “Has Neville never told you why he has been brought up by his grandmother?” he said.

Harry shook his head, wondering, as he did so, how he could have failed to ask Neville this, in almost four years of knowing him.

“Yes, they were talking about Neville’s parents,” said Dumbledore. “His father, **Frank**, was an **Auror** just like Professor Moody. He and his wife were tortured for information about Voldemort’s whereabouts after he lost his powers, as you heard.”

“So they’re dead?” said Harry quietly.

“No,” said Dumbledore, his voice full of a bitterness Harry had never heard there before. “They are **insane**. They are both in **St. Mungo’s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries**. I believe Neville visits them, with his grandmother, during the holidays. They do not recognize him.”

Harry sat there, horror struck. He had never known… never, in four years, bothered to find out…

“The Longbottoms were very popular,” said Dumbledore. “The attacks on them came after **Voldemort’s fall from power**, just when everyone thought they were safe. Those attacks caused a wave of fury such as I have never known. The Ministry was under great pressure to catch those who had done it. Unfortunately, the Longbottoms’ evidence was—given their condition—none too reliable.”

“Then Mr. Crouch’s son might not have been involved?” said Harry slowly.

Dumbledore shook his head.

“As to that, I have no idea.”

Harry sat in silence once more, watching the contents of the Pensieve swirl. There were two more questions he was burning to ask… but they concerned the guilt of living people…

“Er,” he said, “Mr. Bagman…”

“…has never been accused of any Dark activity since,” said Dumbledore calmly.

“Right,” said Harry hastily, staring at the contents of the Pensieve again, which were swirling more slowly now that Dumbledore had stopped adding thoughts. “And… er…” But the Pensieve seemed to be asking his question for him.

**Snape’s face** was swimming on the surface again. Dumbledore glanced down into it, and then up at Harry.

“No more has Professor Snape,” he said.

Harry looked into Dumbledore’s light blue eyes, and the thing he really wanted to know spilled out of his mouth before he could stop it.

“What made you think he’d really stopped supporting Voldemort, Professor?”

Dumbledore held Harry’s gaze for a few seconds, and then said, “That, Harry, is a matter between **Professor Snape** and myself.”

Harry knew that the interview was over; Dumbledore did not look angry, yet there was a finality in his tone that told Harry it was time to go. He stood up, and so did Dumbledore.

“Harry,” he said as Harry reached the door. “Please do not speak about Neville’s parents to anybody else. He has the right to let people know, when he is ready.”

“Yes, Professor,” said Harry, turning to go.

“And—”

Harry looked back. Dumbledore was standing over the Pensieve, his face lit from beneath by its silvery spots of light, looking older than ever. He stared at Harry for a moment, and then said, “Good luck with the **third task**.”

---

## 31. THE THIRD TASK

“**Dumbledore** reckons **You-Know-Who’s** getting stronger again as well?” Ron whispered.

Everything Harry had seen in the Pensieve, nearly everything Dumbledore had told and shown him afterward, he had now shared with Ron and Hermione—and, of course, with Sirius, to whom Harry had sent an owl the moment he had left Dumbledore’s office. Harry, Ron, and Hermione sat up late in the common room once again that night, talking it all over until Harry’s mind was reeling, until he understood what Dumbledore had meant about a head becoming so full of thoughts that it would have been a relief to siphon them off.

Ron stared into the common room fire. Harry thought he saw Ron shiver slightly, even though the evening was warm.

“And he trusts Snape?” Ron said. “He really trusts Snape, even though he knows he was a **Death Eater**?”

“Yes,” said Harry.

Hermione had not spoken for ten minutes. She was sitting with her forehead in her hands, staring at her knees. Harry thought she too looked as though she could have done with a **Pensieve**.

“Rita Skeeter,” she muttered finally.

“How can you be worrying about her now?” said Ron, in utter disbelief.

“I’m not worrying about her,” Hermione said to her knees. “I’m just thinking… remember what she said to me in the Three Broomsticks? ‘I know things about **Ludo Bagman** that would make your hair curl.’ This is what she meant, isn’t it? She reported his trial, she knew he’d passed information to the Death Eaters. And **Winky** too, remember… ‘Ludo Bagman’s a bad wizard.’ Mr. Crouch would have been furious he got off, he would have talked about it at home.”

“Yeah, but Bagman didn’t pass information on purpose, did he?” Hermione shrugged.

“And Fudge reckons **Madame Maxime** attacked Crouch?” Ron said, turning back to Harry.

“Yeah,” said Harry, “but he’s only saying that because Crouch disappeared near the **Beauxbatons carriage**.”

“We never thought of her, did we?” said Ron slowly. “Mind you, she’s definitely got giant blood, and she doesn’t want to admit it—”

“Of course she doesn’t,” said Hermione sharply, looking up. “Look what happened to **Hagrid** when Rita found out about his mother. Look at Fudge, jumping to conclusions about her, just because she’s part giant. Who needs that sort of prejudice? I’d probably say I had big bones if I knew that’s what I’d get for telling the truth.”

Hermione looked at her watch. “We haven’t done any practicing!” she said, looking shocked. “We were going to do the **Impediment Curse**! We’ll have to really get down to it tomorrow! Come on, Harry, you need to get some sleep.”

Harry and Ron went slowly upstairs to their dormitory. As Harry pulled on his pajamas, he looked over at Neville’s bed. True to his word to Dumbledore, he had not told Ron and Hermione about Neville’s parents. As Harry took off his glasses and climbed into his four-poster, he imagined how it must feel to have parents still living but unable to recognize you. He often got sympathy from strangers for being an **orphan**, but as he listened to Neville’s snores, he thought that Neville deserved it more than he did. Lying in the darkness, Harry felt a rush of anger and hate toward the people who had tortured Mr. and Mrs. Longbottom… He remembered the jeers of the crowd as Crouch’s son and his companions had been dragged from the court by the **Dementors**… He understood how they had felt… Then he remembered the milk white face of the screaming boy and realized with a jolt that he had died a year later…

It was **Voldemort**, Harry thought, staring up at the canopy of his bed in the darkness, it all came back to Voldemort… He was the one who had torn these families apart, who had ruined all these lives…

Ron and Hermione were supposed to be studying for their exams, which would finish on the day of the third task, but they were putting most of their efforts into helping Harry prepare.

“Don’t worry about it,” Hermione said shortly when Harry pointed this out to them and said he didn’t mind practicing on his own for a while, “at least we’ll get top marks in **Defense Against the Dark Arts**. We’d never have found out about all these hexes in class.”

“Good training for when we’re all **Aurors**,” said Ron excitedly, attempting the **Impediment Curse** on a wasp that had buzzed into the room and making it stop dead in midair.

The mood in the castle as they entered June became excited and tense again. Everyone was looking forward to the **third task**, which would take place a week before the end of term. Harry was practicing hexes at every available moment. He felt more confident about this task than either of the others. Difficult and dangerous though it would undoubtedly be, Moody was right: Harry had managed to find his way past monstrous creatures and enchanted barriers before now, and this time he had some notice, some chance to prepare himself for what lay ahead.

Tired of walking in on Harry, Hermione, and Ron all over the school, Professor **McGonagall** had given them permission to use the empty **Transfiguration classroom** at lunchtimes. Harry had soon mastered the **Impediment Curse**, a spell to slow down and obstruct attackers; the **Reductor Curse**, which would enable him to blast solid objects out of his way; and the **Four Point Spell**, a useful discovery of Hermione’s that would make his wand point due north, therefore enabling him to check whether he was going in the right direction within the maze. He was still having trouble with the **Shield Charm**, though. This was supposed to cast a temporary, invisible wall around himself that deflected minor curses; Hermione managed to shatter it with a well-placed **Jelly Legs Jinx**, and Harry wobbled around the room for ten minutes afterward before she had looked up the counter jinx.

“You’re still doing really well, though,” Hermione said encouragingly, looking down her list and crossing off those spells they had already learned. “Some of these are bound to come in handy.”

“Come and look at this,” said Ron, who was standing by the window. He was staring down onto the grounds. “What’s Malfoy doing?”

Harry and Hermione went to see. **Malfoy**, **Crabbe**, and **Goyle** were standing in the shadow of a tree below. Crabbe and Goyle seemed to be keeping a lookout; both were smirking. Malfoy was holding his hand up to his mouth and speaking into it.

“He looks like he’s using a walkie talkie,” said Harry curiously.

“He can’t be,” said Hermione, “I’ve told you, those sorts of things don’t work around Hogwarts. Come on, Harry,” she added briskly, turning away from the window and moving back into the middle of the room, “let’s try that Shield Charm again.”

Sirius was sending daily owls now. Like Hermione, he seemed to want to concentrate on getting Harry through the last task before they concerned themselves with anything else. He reminded Harry in every letter that whatever might be going on outside the walls of Hogwarts was not Harry’s responsibility, nor was it within his power to influence it.

If **Voldemort** is really getting stronger again, he wrote, my priority is to ensure your safety. He cannot hope to lay hands on you while you are under **Dumbledore’s protection**, but all the same, take no risks: Concentrate on getting through that **maze** safely, and then we can turn our attention to other matters.

## Third Task Preparation

Harry’s nerves mounted as **June the twenty fourth** drew closer, but they were not as bad as those he had felt before the first and second tasks. For one thing, he was confident that, this time, he had done everything in his power to prepare for the task. For another, this was the **final hurdle**, and however well or badly he did, the tournament would at last be over, which would be an enormous relief.

## Breakfast at Gryffindor Table

Breakfast was a very noisy affair at the **Gryffindor table** on the morning of the third task. The **post owls** appeared, bringing Harry a good luck card from **Sirius**. It was only a piece of parchment, folded over and bearing a muddy paw print on its front, but Harry appreciated it all the same.

A **screech owl** arrived for Hermione, carrying her morning copy of the **Daily Prophet** as usual. She unfolded the paper, glanced at the front page, and spat out a mouthful of pumpkin juice all over it.

### Reaction to the Daily Prophet

- Harry and Ron asked, “What?”
- Hermione tried to hide the paper but Ron grabbed it and saw the headline.
- Ron said, “No way. Not today. That old cow.”
- Harry questioned if it was about him; Ron gave an unconvincing denial.
- Then Draco Malfoy shouted, mocking Harry from the Slytherin table with a copy of the **Daily Prophet**.

### The Headline: **HARRY POTTER “DISTURBED AND DANGEROUS”**

The article by **Rita Skeeter, Special Correspondent**, declares:

- Harry, the boy who defeated **He-Who-Must-Not-Be-Named**, is unstable and possibly dangerous.
- Harry **regularly collapses at school** and complains of pain in his scar (a relic of the curse from **You-Know-Who**).
- During a **Divination lesson**, Harry stormed out because his scar was hurting.
- Experts at **St. Mungo’s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries** suggest Harry’s brain might be affected by the attack.
- Some speculate Harry may be **pretending** as a plea for attention.

### Allegations and Accusations

The article also claims that:

- **Albus Dumbledore**, Headmaster of Hogwarts, has concealed worrying facts about Harry.
- Harry can speak **Parseltongue**, the ability to converse with snakes, considered a **Dark Art**.
- Draco Malfoy states Harry has made friends with **werewolves and giants**, hinting at his desire for power.
- A member of the **Dark Force Defense League** expressed suspicion about anyone who can speak Parseltongue or associates with werewolves and giants.
- Concerns arise that Harry might resort to the **Dark Arts** during the Triwizard Tournament.

### Reactions at the Gryffindor Table

- Harry mocks the article as “gone off me a bit.”
- Malfoy, Crabbe, and Goyle mock Harry, mimicking snake-like gestures.
- Ron is surprised that Skeeter knew about Harry’s scar hurting during Divination.
- Harry explains the window was open when he left to breathe.
- Hermione is puzzled; she tries to research Skeeter’s magical methods of bugging.

### Hermione’s Suspicion and Departure

- Hermione has an idea that Skeeter must have accessed the window ledge magically.
- She rushes out to the library to confirm her suspicions, risking missing her **History of Magic exam**.
- Ron comments on Hermione’s dedication to exposing Skeeter.

## Champions’ Gathering

- Professor McGonagall informs Harry that the champions are meeting in the chamber off the Hall after breakfast.
- The task is in the evening, but champions are to greet their families, who are invited to watch the final task.
- Harry worries the **Dursleys** might attend but doubts it.

### In the Chamber

- Harry sees **Cedric** and his parents, **Viktor Krum** with his Bulgarian parents, and **Fleur Delacour** with her mother and sister.
- **Mrs. Weasley** and **Bill** surprise Harry by coming to watch him.
- Mrs. Weasley kisses Harry on the cheek; Bill congratulates him on his performance against the **Horntail**.

### Conversation in the Chamber

- Fleur shows interest in Bill’s long hair and earrings.
- Harry thanks Mrs. Weasley and mentions his worries about the Dursleys.
- Mrs. Weasley hints at her disdain for the Dursleys.

### Nostalgia and Tour

- Bill reminisces about the chamber and asks about **Sir Cadogan**, a mad knight portrait.
- Mrs. Weasley mentions the **Fat Lady** and shares a story about getting a telling off for being out late.
- Bill asks for a tour, which Harry agrees to give.

### Encounter with Amos Diggory

- Amos Diggory criticizes Harry for losing points to Cedric.
- Cedric tells Harry Amos is angry about **Rita Skeeter’s** incorrect article claiming Harry was the only Hogwarts champion.
- Mrs. Weasley defends Harry and criticizes Skeeter.
- Amos’s wife calms him down and they leave.

## Morning Walk with Bill and Mrs. Weasley

- Harry enjoys walking around the sunny grounds showing Bill and Mrs. Weasley the **Beauxbatons carriage** and the **Durmstrang ship**.
- Mrs. Weasley shows interest in the **Whomping Willow**, planted after her time.
- She reminisces about the previous gamekeeper, **Ogg**.

### Personal News

- Harry asks about **Percy**.
- Bill replies, “Not good.”

## Triwizard Tournament: The Third Task

### Ministry Concerns and Percy’s Strain

“He’s very upset,” said **Mrs. Weasley**, lowering her voice and glancing around. “The **Ministry** wants to keep **Mr. Crouch’s disappearance** quiet, but **Percy**’s been hauled in for questioning about the instructions **Mr. Crouch** has been sending in. They seem to think there’s a chance they weren’t genuinely written by him. Percy’s been under a lot of strain. They’re not letting him fill in for Mr. Crouch as the fifth judge tonight. **Cornelius Fudge** is going to be doing it.”

---

### Lunch at the Castle

They returned to the castle for lunch.

“Mum—Bill!” said **Ron**, looking stunned, as he joined the Gryffindor table. “What’re you doing here?”

“Come to watch **Harry** in the last task!” said **Mrs. Weasley** brightly. “I must say, it makes a lovely change, not having to cook. How was your exam?”

“Oh… okay,” said Ron. “Couldn’t remember all the goblin rebels’ names, so I invented a few. It’s all right,” he said, helping himself to a Cornish pasty, while Mrs. Weasley looked stern, “they’re all called stuff like **Bodrod the Bearded** and **Urg the Unclean**; it wasn’t hard.”

**Fred, George,** and **Ginny** came to sit next to them too, and Harry was having such a good time he felt almost as though he were back at the **Burrow**; he had forgotten to worry about that evening’s task.  

Not until **Hermione** turned up, halfway through lunch, did he remember that she had had a brainwave about **Rita Skeeter**.

---

### Interaction Between Hermione and Mrs. Weasley

“Are you going to tell us—?” Hermione shook her head warningly and glanced at Mrs. Weasley.

“Hello, Hermione,” said Mrs. Weasley, much more stiffly than usual.

“Hello,” said Hermione, her smile faltering at the cold expression on Mrs. Weasley’s face.

Harry looked between them, then said, “Mrs. Weasley, you didn’t believe that rubbish Rita Skeeter wrote in **Witch Weekly**, did you? Because Hermione’s not my girlfriend.”

“Oh!” said Mrs. Weasley “No—of course I didn’t!” But she became considerably warmer toward Hermione after that.

---

### Afternoon Walk and Evening Feast

Harry, Bill, and Mrs. Weasley whiled away the afternoon with a long walk around the castle, then returned to the **Great Hall** for the evening feast.  

**Ludo Bagman** and **Cornelius Fudge** had joined the staff table. Bagman looked quite cheerful, but Fudge, sitting next to **Madame Maxime**, looked stern and silent. Madame Maxime was concentrating on her plate, and Harry thought her eyes looked red. **Hagrid** kept glancing along the table at her.

There were more courses than usual, but Harry, feeling really nervous now, didn’t eat much. As the enchanted ceiling began to fade from blue to a dusky purple, **Dumbledore** rose to his feet and silence fell.

---

### Announcement of the Final Task

“Ladies and gentlemen, in five minutes’ time, I will be asking you to make your way down to the **Quidditch field** for the third and final task of the **Triwizard Tournament**. Will the champions please follow **Mr. Bagman** down to the stadium now.”

Harry got up. The **Gryffindors** applauded him; the Weasleys and Hermione all wished him good luck. He headed out of the Great Hall with **Cedric**, **Fleur**, and **Viktor**.

---

### On the Way to the Maze

“Feeling all right, Harry?” Bagman asked.

“Confident?” 

“I’m okay,” said Harry. He was nervous but kept running through hexes and spells he had been practicing, which steadied him.

The Quidditch field was unrecognizable. A **twenty-foot-high hedge** ran all around the edge of it, with a gap in front of them leading to the vast **maze**. The passage beyond looked dark and creepy.

---

### Maze Atmosphere and Safety Instructions

Five minutes later, the stands filled with excited voices and rumbling feet. The sky was deep blue, with the first stars starting to appear.  

**Hagrid, Professor Moody, Professor McGonagall,** and **Professor Flitwick** arrived wearing large, red luminous stars on their hats except Hagrid, who had his on his moleskin vest.

Professor McGonagall explained:

- They would patrol the outside of the maze.
- If a champion got into difficulty, they should send red sparks into the air for rescue.

The champions nodded.

---

### Start of the Final Task

“Off you go, then!” said Bagman, and the patrollers went their ways.

Bagman pointed his wand at his throat, muttered, “Sonorus,” and his magically magnified voice echoed:

“Ladies and gentlemen, the third and final task of the Triwizard Tournament is about to begin!

- **Tied for first place** with 85 points each: **Cedric Diggory** and **Harry Potter**, both of Hogwarts!
- **Second place**, 80 points: **Viktor Krum**, of Durmstrang Institute.
- **Third place**: **Fleur Delacour**, of Beauxbatons Academy.”

Cheers and applause filled the stands. Harry saw his family and friends applauding Fleur politely.

---

### Entering the Maze

“So… on my whistle, Harry and Cedric!” said Bagman.

“Three—two—one—”

A short blast on the whistle sent Harry and Cedric hurrying into the maze.

The towering hedges cast black shadows and silenced the crowd noise. Harry felt almost underwater. He pulled out his wand and whispered, “Lumos,” hearing Cedric do the same behind him.

After about fifty yards, they reached a fork. They looked at each other.

“See you,” Harry said, taking the left path; Cedric took the right.

---

### Progress Through the Maze

Bagman’s whistle blew—the sound marking Viktor’s entrance. All champions were inside.

Harry felt the old sensation of being watched. The maze darkened under the deepening navy sky.

At a second fork, Harry whispered, “Point Me,” to his wand holding it flat in his palm.

The wand pointed right, into a solid hedge. He needed northwest, so he took the left fork, planning to turn right soon after.

The path was empty and unblocked, which unnerved Harry. He expected to confront obstacles by now.

---

### Encounters in the Maze

Suddenly, Harry heard movement behind him and held his wand ready. Cedric appeared, shaken, with a smoking sleeve.

“Hagrid’s **Blast-Ended Skrewts**!” Cedric hissed. “They’re enormous—I only just got away!” Cedric disappeared down another path.

Harry hurried on, then saw a **Dementor** gliding toward him—twelve feet tall, hooded, with scabbed hands and rattling breath.

He summoned a happy thought of escaping the maze and celebrating with Ron and Hermione, then raised his wand and cried, “**Expecto Patronum!**”

A silver stag erupted and galloped toward the Dementor, which stumbled. Never before had Harry seen a Dementor trip.

“Hang on!” Harry shouted, advancing. “You’re a **Boggart**! **Riddikulus!**”

The shape shifter exploded in a wisp of smoke. The silver stag faded. Harry wished the Patronus could have stayed for company but moved on quietly.

---

### Navigating Further Obstacles

Harry turned left, right, left again, encountering dead ends twice. Using the **Four Point Spell**, he realized he was going too far east. He turned back, took a right turn, and saw an odd golden mist ahead.

He pointed his wand’s beam cautiously at the mist. It looked like an enchantment.

He tried, “Reducio!” but the mist remained. The Reductor Curse worked on solids.

He hesitated to enter the mist when a scream shattered the silence.

“Fleur?” Harry yelled.

There was silence. He took a deep breath and ran through the enchanted mist.

---

### The Upside-Down World

The world turned upside down. Harry hung from the ground, hair on end, glasses dangling off his nose, threatening to fall into the bottomless sky.

He clutched his glasses and felt as if his feet were glued to the grass that was now the ceiling. Below stretched the dark, starry heavens—endless.

He thought hard—none of his practiced spells accounted for reversed gravity.

He had two choices:

- Try to move despite the risk.
- Send up red sparks and be rescued, which meant disqualification.

---

### Overcoming the Gravity Reversal

He shut his eyes to block the dizzying view, then pulled his right foot hard from the grassy ceiling.

Immediately, the world righted itself. Harry fell forward onto his knees on solid ground, limp with shock.

After steadying himself, he got up and hurried away from the golden mist, which twinkled innocently in the moonlight.

---

### Searching for Fleur and Moving On

Harry paused at a junction, searching for signs of Fleur. He was sure she had screamed.

There was no sign of red sparks—meaning either she had escaped on her own or was too incapacitated to signal.

Feeling uneasy, Harry took the right fork and thought silently, **One champion down...**

## The Maze Challenge

The **cup** was somewhere close by, and it sounded as though **Fleur** was no longer in the running. He’d got this far, hadn’t he? What if he actually managed to **win**? Fleetingly, and for the first time since he’d found himself **champion**, he saw again that image of himself, raising the **Triwizard Cup** in front of the rest of the school.

He met nothing for ten minutes, but kept running into **dead ends**. Twice he took the same wrong turning. Finally, he found a new route and started to jog along it, his **wandlight waving**, making his shadow flicker and distort on the hedge walls. Then he rounded another corner and found himself facing a **Blast-Ended Skrewt**.

### Encounter with the Blast-Ended Skrewt

Cedric was right—it was **enormous**. Ten feet long, it looked more like a giant scorpion than anything. Its long sting was curled over its back. Its thick **armor** glinted in the light from Harry’s wand, which he pointed at it.

- “**Stupefy!**”  
The spell hit the skrewt’s armor and rebounded; Harry ducked just in time, but could smell **burning hair**; it had singed the top of his head.  
- The skrewt issued a blast of fire from its end and flew forward toward him.  
- “**Impedimenta!**” Harry yelled. The spell hit the skrewt’s armor again and ricocheted off; Harry staggered back a few paces and fell over.  
- “**IMPEDIMENTA!**”

The skrewt was inches from him when it froze—he had managed to hit it on its **fleshy, shell-less underside**. Panting, Harry pushed himself away and ran in the opposite direction—the **Impediment Curse** was not permanent; the skrewt would regain the use of its legs soon.

### Navigating the Maze

He took a left path and hit a **dead end**, then a right, and hit another. Forcing himself to stop, heart hammering, he performed the **Four Point Spell** again, backtracked, and chose a path that would take him **northwest**.

He had been hurrying along the new path for a few minutes when he heard something in the path running parallel that made him stop dead.

## The Attack on Cedric

- “What are you doing?” yelled **Cedric’s voice**.  
- “What the hell d’you think you’re doing?”  
- Then Harry heard **Krum’s voice** shouting “**Crucio!**”

The air was suddenly full of Cedric’s yells. Horrified, Harry began sprinting, trying to find a way into Cedric’s path. When none appeared, he tried the **Reductor Curse** again. It wasn’t very effective but burned a small hole in the hedge. Harry forced his leg through, kicking at thick brambles until they broke. He struggled through, tearing his robes, and looked to his right to see **Cedric jerking and twitching** on the ground, with **Krum standing over him**.

Harry pulled himself up and pointed his wand at Krum just as Krum looked up. Krum turned and began to run.

- “**Stupefy!**” Harry yelled.  
  The spell hit Krum in the back; he stopped, fell forward, and lay motionless, facedown in the grass.

Harry dashed over to Cedric, who had stopped twitching and was lying there panting, hands over his face.

- “Are you all right?” Harry said roughly, grabbing Cedric’s arm.  
- “Yeah,” panted Cedric. “Yeah… I don’t believe it… he crept up behind me… I heard him, I turned around, and he had his wand on me…” Cedric got up, still shaking.  

He and Harry looked down at Krum.

- “I can’t believe this… I thought he was all right,” Harry said, staring at Krum.  
- “So did I,” said Cedric.

- “Did you hear Fleur scream earlier?” said Harry.  
- “Yeah,” said Cedric. “You don’t think Krum got her too?”  
- “I don’t know,” said Harry slowly.

- “Should we leave him here?” Cedric muttered.  
- “No,” said Harry. “I reckon we should send up red sparks. Someone’ll come and collect him… otherwise he’ll probably be eaten by a skrewt.”  
- “He’d deserve it,” Cedric muttered, but all the same, he raised his wand and shot a shower of **red sparks** into the air, which hovered above Krum, marking the spot.

Harry and Cedric stood there in the darkness, looking around them. Then Cedric said, “Well… I s’pose we’d better go on…”

- “What?” said Harry. “Oh… yeah… right…”

It was an odd moment. He and Cedric had been briefly united against Krum—now the fact that they were **opponents** came back to Harry. The two proceeded up the dark path without speaking, then Harry turned left and Cedric right. Cedric’s footsteps soon died away.

## Continuing the Maze

Harry moved on, continuing to use the **Four Point Spell**, ensuring he was moving in the right direction. It was now between him and Cedric. His desire to reach the cup first burned stronger than ever, but he could hardly believe what he’d just seen Krum do. The use of an **Unforgivable Curse** on a fellow human meant a life in **Azkaban**, that was what Moody had told them.

- Krum surely couldn’t have wanted the **Triwizard Cup** that badly…

Harry sped up. Every so often, he hit more **dead ends**, but the increasing darkness made him feel sure he was nearing the **heart of the maze**.

### Encounter with the Sphinx

As he strode down a long, straight path, he saw movement. His beam of wandlight hit an extraordinary creature, one which he had only seen in pictures in the **Monster Book of Monsters**.

- It was a **sphinx** with the body of an oversized lion and the head of a woman.  
- She turned her almond-shaped eyes upon Harry and paced side to side, blocking his progress.  
- She spoke in a deep, hoarse voice:  
  “You are very near your goal. The quickest way is past me.”

Harry asked if she would move.

- She replied she would **only** move if he answered her **riddle** correctly.  
- Answer on first guess—he could pass; answer wrongly—she would attack; remain silent—he could walk away unscathed.

Harry felt unsure, knowing **Hermione** was better at riddles.

- “Okay,” he said. “Can I hear the riddle?”

The sphinx sat in the middle of the path and recited:

> First think of the person who lives in disguise,  
> Who deals in secrets and tells naught but lies.  
> Next, tell me what’s always the last thing to mend,  
> The middle of middle and end of the end?  
> And finally give me the sound often heard  
> During the search for a hard to find word.  
> Now string them together, and answer me this,  
> Which creature would you be unwilling to kiss?”

Harry asked her to repeat the riddle slowly. She did.

Harry pondered:

- A **person in disguise** who lies might be a **spy**.  
- He struggled with the next clue and asked her to repeat it.  
- Finally, he realized the “sound often heard during the search”—“**er**!”

Harry guessed the answer was **“spider.”**

The sphinx smiled broadly, got up, stretched her front legs, and moved aside for him to pass.

“Thanks!” said Harry, amazed at his own brilliance, and dashed forward.

## The Final Stretch

Harry’s wand confirmed he was on course. As long as he didn’t face anything horrible, he might have a chance.

He broke into a run and chose a path to the right. Ahead, he saw the **Triwizard Cup** gleaming a hundred yards away.

### Final Confrontation

Suddenly, a dark figure hurtled onto the path.

- **Cedric** was sprinting toward the cup, much faster than Harry.  
- Then Harry saw something immense moving quickly over a hedge to his left, intersecting his path.  

He yelled:

- “**Cedric! On your left!**”  
Cedric barely avoided colliding but tripped and dropped his wand as a **gigantic spider** stepped into the path and bore down on him.

Harry yelled:

- “**Stupefy!**” but the spell barely affected the spider.  
- The spider scuttled around and ran at Harry instead.

He cast spells repeatedly:

- “**Stupefy! Impedimenta! Stupefy!**”  
The spider was either too large or magical for the spells to work; Harry glimpsed eight shining black eyes and razor-sharp pincers before it was upon him.

Harry was lifted into the air in its front legs, struggling madly.

- He kicked its pincers, causing sharp pain.  
- Cedric yelled “**Stupefy!**” too, but still no effect.  
- Harry shouted “**Expelliarmus!**”

The **Disarming Spell** made the spider drop him, causing him to fall twelve feet onto his injured leg, which crumpled beneath him.

Without pause, he aimed at the spider’s **underbelly** and shouted “**Stupefy!**” just as Cedric yelled the same.

The two spells combined:

- The spider keeled over sideways, flattening a nearby hedge.  
- The path was strewn with a tangle of hairy legs.

### After the Battle

Harry heard Cedric shout:

- “**Harry! You all right? Did it fall on you?**”  
- Harry called back, panting, looking down at his **bleeding leg**.  
- Thick, gluey secretion from the spider’s pincers coated his torn robes.  

He tried to get up but needed support. Leaning against the hedge, gasping, he looked around.

Cedric was standing feet from the **Triwizard Cup**, gleaming behind him.

Harry said:

- “**Take it, then. Go on, take it. You’re there.**”

But Cedric didn’t move.

- He looked at Harry, then the cup, longing in his eyes.  
- He took a deep breath.

“You take it. You should win. That’s twice you’ve saved my neck in here.”

Harry felt angry; his leg was painful and aching all over. After all his efforts, Cedric had beaten him to it, just as he had beaten Harry to ask **Cho to the ball**.

- “That’s not how it’s supposed to work,” Harry said. “The one who reaches the cup first gets the points. That’s you. I’m not going to win any races on this leg.”

Cedric shook his head, stepping nearer the stunned spider, away from the cup.

- “No,” he said.

## 32. FLESH, BLOOD, AND BONE

“Stop being **noble**,” said **Harry** irritably. “Just take it, then we can get out of here.” **Cedric** watched **Harry** steadying himself, holding tight to the hedge.

“You told me about the **dragons**,” Cedric said. “I would’ve gone down in the **first task** if you hadn’t told me what was coming.”

“I had help on that too,” Harry snapped, trying to mop up his **bloody leg** with his robes. “You helped me with the **egg**—we’re square.”

“I had help on the egg in the first place,” said Cedric.

“We’re still square,” said Harry, testing his leg gingerly; it shook violently as he put weight on it; he had **sprained his ankle** when the **spider** had dropped him.

“You should’ve got more **points** on the **second task**,” said Cedric mulishly. “You stayed behind to get all the hostages. I should’ve done that.”

“I was the only one who was thick enough to take that **song** seriously!” said Harry bitterly. “Just take the cup!”

“No,” said Cedric.

He stepped over the spider’s tangled legs to join Harry, who stared at him. Cedric was serious. He was walking away from the sort of **glory** **Hufflepuff House** hadn’t had in centuries.

“Go on,” Cedric said. He looked as though this was costing him every ounce of **resolution** he had, but his face was set, his arms were folded, he seemed decided.

Harry looked from Cedric to the cup. For one shining moment, he saw himself emerging from the maze, holding it. He saw himself holding the **Triwizard Cup** aloft, heard the roar of the crowd, saw **Cho’s face** shining with admiration, more clearly than he had ever seen it before… and then the picture faded, and he found himself staring at Cedric’s shadowy, stubborn face.

“Both of us,” Harry said.

“What?”

“We’ll take it at the same time. It’s still a **Hogwarts victory**. We’ll tie for it.” Cedric stared at Harry. He unfolded his arms.

“You—you sure?”

“Yeah,” said Harry. “Yeah… we’ve helped each other out, haven’t we? We both got here. Let’s just take it together.”

For a moment, Cedric looked as though he couldn’t believe his ears; then his face split in a grin.

“You’re on,” he said. “Come here.”

He grabbed Harry’s arm below the shoulder and helped Harry limp toward the plinth where the cup stood. When they had reached it, they both held a hand out over one of the cup’s gleaming handles.

“On three, right?” said Harry. “One—two—three—”

He and Cedric both grasped a handle.

Instantly, Harry felt a jerk somewhere behind his navel. His feet had left the ground. He could not unclench the hand holding the **Triwizard Cup**; it was pulling him onward in a howl of wind and swirling color, Cedric at his side.

---

Harry felt his feet slam into the ground; his injured leg gave way, and he fell forward; his hand let go of the **Triwizard Cup** at last. He raised his head.

“Where are we?” he said.

Cedric shook his head. He got up, pulled Harry to his feet, and they looked around.

They had left the **Hogwarts grounds** completely; they had obviously traveled miles—perhaps hundreds of miles—for even the mountains surrounding the castle were gone. They were standing instead in a dark and overgrown **graveyard**; the black outline of a small church was visible beyond a large **yew tree** to their right. A hill rose above them to their left. Harry could just make out the outline of a fine old **house** on the hillside.

Cedric looked down at the **Triwizard Cup** and then up at Harry.

“Did anyone tell you the cup was a **Portkey**?” he asked.

“Nope,” said Harry. He was looking around the graveyard. It was completely silent and slightly eerie. “Is this supposed to be part of the task?”

“I dunno,” said Cedric. He sounded slightly nervous. “Wands out, d’you reckon?”

“Yeah,” said Harry, glad that Cedric had made the suggestion rather than him.

They pulled out their **wands**. Harry kept looking around him. He had, yet again, the strange feeling that they were being **watched**.

“Someone’s coming,” he said suddenly.

Squinting tensely through the darkness, they watched the figure drawing nearer, walking steadily toward them between the graves. Harry couldn’t make out a face, but from the way it was walking and holding its arms, he could tell that it was carrying something. Whoever it was, he was short, and wearing a **hooded cloak** pulled up over his head to obscure his face. And—several paces nearer, the gap between them closing all the time—Harry saw that the thing in the person's arms looked like a **baby**

## Resurrection of Lord Voldemort

**"B - blood of the enemy… forcibly taken… you will… resurrect your foe."**

Harry was tied tightly and could do nothing. He saw the shining silver dagger in **Wormtail’s** hand penetrate his right arm, and blood seeped down his torn robes. Wormtail collected Harry’s blood in a glass vial.

Wormtail poured the blood into the cauldron. Instantly, the liquid turned blinding white. Afterward, Wormtail collapsed, clutching his bleeding arm. The cauldron shimmered with bright sparks, turning everything velvety black around Harry.

Suddenly, the sparks ceased, and a thick white steam billowed, obscuring everything. Harry hoped the ritual had failed.

Through the mist, Harry saw a **tall, skeletally thin man** rising from the cauldron.

**“Robe me,”** whispered the cold, high voice. Wormtail sobbed but pulled black robes over the man’s head.

The man stepped out, revealing a **face whiter than a skull, with wide scarlet eyes and a flat snake-like nose**.

**Lord Voldemort had risen again.**

---

## 33. THE DEATH EATERS

Voldemort examined his body. His **hands were like pale spiders**, and his red eyes gleamed with slit pupils. Ignoring Wormtail and the circling snake, Voldemort drew his wand.

He struck Wormtail against a headstone and laughed a cold, mirthless laugh at Harry.

Wormtail pleaded, **“My Lord… you promised…”**

Voldemort ordered, **“Hold out your arm.”**

Wormtail extended his bleeding stump, but Voldemort demanded, **“The other arm, Wormtail.”**

Harry saw a vivid red tattoo on Wormtail’s left arm, the **Dark Mark** from the Quidditch World Cup sky. Voldemort pressed his finger to it, turning the mark **jet black**. The scar on Harry’s forehead burned sharply.

Voldemort whispered:

- **“How many will be brave enough to return when they feel it?”**
- **“And how many will be foolish enough to stay away?”**

He paced, facing the dark graveyard. Then he smiled cruelly at Harry:

**“You stand, Harry Potter, upon the remains of my late father. A Muggle and a fool… very like your dear mother.”**

Voldemort recounted his family history:

- His mother, a witch, was abandoned by his Muggle father.
- His mother died giving birth to him.
- He was raised in a Muggle orphanage.
- He vowed vengeance on his father, **Tom Riddle**.

---

## Return of the Death Eaters

Suddenly, cloaks swished as masked and hooded **wizards Apparated** from shadows.

One by one, they approached Voldemort on their knees, kissing the hem of his black robes.

They formed a circle around Voldemort, Harry, Wormtail, and the grave of **Tom Riddle**. Gaps in the circle suggested waiting for more.

Voldemort addressed them quietly:

- **“Welcome, Death Eaters. Thirteen years since we last met.”**
- **“Are we still united under the Dark Mark?”**

He sniffed the air.

**“I smell guilt.”**

Shivers ran through the circle. No one spoke except Wormtail, still sobbing.

Voldemort accused them:

- They believed him broken or gone.
- They slipped back among his enemies.
- They pleaded innocence, ignorance, or bewitchment.
- They may have pledged loyalty to the great wizard **Albus Dumbledore**.

The mention of **Dumbledore** caused murmurs and head shakes, but Voldemort ignored them.

---

## Disloyalty and Punishment

Suddenly, one Death Eater collapsed at Voldemort’s feet, begging forgiveness.

Voldemort laughed and cast **“Crucio”**, causing the man to writhe and shriek.

He then said:

- **“Thirteen years' repayment before forgiveness.”**
- Wormtail had paid some of the debt through suffering.
- Wormtail returned out of fear, not loyalty.

Voldemort rewarded Wormtail. He raised his wand and created a **gleaming silver hand** that seamlessly attached to Wormtail’s stump.

Wormtail gasped in disbelief.

**“Master… it is beautiful… thank you…”**

Voldemort commanded Wormtail's loyalty:

**“May your loyalty never waver again, Wormtail.”**

Wormtail nodded, still tearful.

---

## Confrontation with Lucius Malfoy

Voldemort approached the man on Wormtail’s right.

**“Lucius, my slippery friend,”** he whispered:

- Lucius appeared respectable to the world.
- Voldemort accused him of not aiding his master.
- Voldemort referred to Lucius’s involvement in **Muggle torture** and the **Quidditch World Cup**.

Lucius replied:

**“Had there been any sign, I would have been at your side immediately.”**

Voldemort interrupted:

**“And yet you ran from my Mark last summer.”**

Lucius fell silent.

Voldemort disappointedly declared:

**“I expect more faithful service in the future.”**

## Voldemort’s Return and the Death Eaters’ Assembly

“Of course, my Lord, of course… You are **merciful**, thank you…”

Voldemort moved on, stopping to stare at a space large enough for two people, separating **Malfoy** and the next man.

### The Lestranges and Azkaban

- “The **Lestranges** should stand here,” said Voldemort quietly.
- They are **entombed in Azkaban**.
- They were **faithful** and chose Azkaban rather than renounce Voldemort.
- When Azkaban is broken open, the Lestranges will be **honored beyond their dreams**.
- The **Dementors** will join them as **natural allies**.
- Voldemort plans to **recall the banished giants** and have all devoted servants returned.
- He will assemble an **army of creatures whom all fear**.

### Interactions With Death Eaters

Voldemort passed some Death Eaters in silence but paused before others:

- **Macnair**: Destroying dangerous beasts for the Ministry of Magic, told by Wormtail. Voldemort promises better victims soon.
- Macnair responds, “Thank you, Master… thank you.”

He next approached the two largest hooded figures:

- **Crabbe** and **Goyle** were addressed; they bowed clumsily and muttered affirmations.
- **Nott**, a stooped figure near Mr. Goyle's shadow, vowed his faithfulness. Voldemort dismissed prolonged declarations.

### Missing Death Eaters

Voldemort surveyed the largest gap in the circle:

- Six **missing Death Eaters**:
  - Three dead in his service.
  - One cowardly retreating, who will pay.
  - One believed gone forever, who will be killed.
  - One **most faithful servant** who has reentered service.
  
The Death Eaters exchanged glances behind their masks.

### Harry Potter’s Role

- The faithful servant is **at Hogwarts**.
- Through this servant’s efforts, **Harry Potter** arrived tonight.
- Voldemort calls Harry his **"guest of honor"** at his rebirthing party.

## Voldemort’s Explanation for His Return

A Death Eater beside Wormtail, in **Lucius Malfoy’s voice**, begged Voldemort to explain his return.

Voldemort replied:

- The story **begins and ends** with Harry Potter.
- Harry is known as Voldemort’s **downfall**.
- Voldemort attempted to kill Harry, but Harry’s mother’s **sacrifice left him protected**.
- Voldemort admits he was **foolish to overlook** this **old magic**.
- He can **touch Harry now**, demonstrated by a painful touch to Harry’s cheek.

### Voldemort’s State After His Fall

- The killing curse was **deflected** by Harry’s mother’s sacrifice, rebounding on Voldemort.
- Voldemort was **ripped from his body**, reduced to less than spirit or ghost.
- Despite this, he was **still alive**, but powerless and wandless.
- He forced himself to **exist sleeplessly, endlessly**.
- Settled in a **faraway forest** awaiting rescue.
- He had no one to perform the magic necessary to restore him.

### Possession and Weakness

- His only remaining power was to **possess bodies**.
- He avoided humans due to the **Aurors’ vigilance**.
- He sometimes inhabited animals like **snakes**, but these bodies were unsuitable for magic and short-lived.
- About **four years ago**, a **young wizard** at Dumbledore’s school helped him return.
- Voldemort possessed this wizard’s body, but the plan failed to steal the **Sorcerer’s Stone**.
- Voldemort was thwarted again by Harry Potter.

### Death Eaters’ Loyalty and Regeneration

- The possessed wizard died, leaving Voldemort as weak as before.
- He almost lost hope of regaining power or being helped by Death Eaters.
- Then, **Wormtail** returned after faking his death.
- Wormtail was driven from hiding by former allies and sought Voldemort in an Albanian forest.

### Wormtail and Bertha Jorkins

- Wormtail stopped at an inn and met **Bertha Jorkins** of the Ministry of Magic.
- Wormtail manipulated Bertha to accompany him and overpowered her.
- Bertha became a source of invaluable **information**.
- She revealed the **Triwizard Tournament** would take place at Hogwarts.
- She revealed a faithful Death Eater could aid Voldemort.
